#Supplementary Data

#List of 2156 mutations for assessment of computational methods for predicting protein stabilty upon mutation

#When using this set of mutations in your study please cite the original article:
#Potapov V., Cohen, M. & Schreiber, G. (2009). Assessing computational methods for predicting protein stability upon mutation: good on average but not in the details. Protein Eng. Des. Sel.; doi: 10.1093/protein/gzp030. [Abstract]  [Full text]
#As described in the paper, this dataset of mutations was composed from the list of 964 mutations (Guerois et al., 2002; PubMed) and the list of 2972 mutations from the ProTherm database (Kumar et al., 2006; PubMed).

#Legend
#    No.     serial number
#    PBD     PDB ID and chain identifier of the wild type structure
#    WT      wild type residue
#    MUT     mutant residue
#    RN      residue sequence number
#    ddG_exp experimentally measured change in protein stability
#    NM      number of measurements (if >1 then average ddG_exp value was calculated)

#Note
#    The first column for each method shows predicted ddG.
#    The second column idicates whether mutation was used in evaluating the method (1) or not (0). Refer to the original paper for details.
